Calculation Trail (every step, every number)
Step 1 — Pi Ratings
formula: composite = (home_rating + away_rating) / 2
Mexico: home_rating=-0.0295, away_rating=0.0029 → composite = (-0.0295 + 0.0029) / 2 = -0.0133 (from 8 matches)
South Korea: home_rating=-0.2005, away_rating=0.0200 → composite = (-0.2005 + 0.0200) / 2 = -0.0902 (from 8 matches)
Step 2 — Calibration Parameters
total_anchor = 3.1538 (fitted, n=26 2026 matches)
rho = -0.2000 (fitted) — Dixon-Coles low-score correlation
Step 3 — Lambdas (Expected Goals per Team)
formula: margin = home_composite − away_composite
formula: λ_H = max(0.30, total_anchor/2 + margin/2)
formula: λ_A = max(0.30, total_anchor/2 − margin/2)
margin = -0.0133 − -0.0902 = 0.0770
λ_H = max(0.30, 3.1538/2 + 0.0770/2) = 1.6154
λ_A = max(0.30, 3.1538/2 − 0.0770/2) = 1.5384
Step 4 — Dixon-Coles PMF Grid (26×26)
formula: P(h,a) = τ(h,a,ρ) × Poisson(h; λ_H) × Poisson(a; λ_A), then normalise
τ(0,0)=1−λ_H×λ_A×ρ, τ(1,0)=1+λ_A×ρ, τ(0,1)=1+λ_H×ρ, τ(1,1)=1−ρ, τ(h,a)=1 for h+a≥2
With λ_H=1.6154, λ_A=1.5384, ρ=-0.2000:
τ(0,0) = 1 − 1.6154×1.5384×(-0.2000) = 1.4970
Grid sum = 1.000000 (should be ≈1.000000)
E[home goals] = 1.6154, E[away goals] = 1.5384
Step 5 — Market Derivations (cell summation)
home_win = Σ P(h,a) for h > a = 0.3773
draw = Σ P(h,a) for h = a = 0.2785
away_win = Σ P(h,a) for h < a = 0.3442
over_2.5 = Σ P(h,a) for h+a > 2.5 = 0.6104
btts_yes = Σ P(h,a) for h≥1 AND a≥1 = 0.6504

Step 3 — Lambdas (Expected Goals per Team)
formula: margin = home_composite − away_composite
formula: λ_H = max(0.30, total_anchor/2 + margin/2)
formula: λ_A = max(0.30, total_anchor/2 − margin/2)
margin = -0.1950 − -0.2905 = 0.0955
λ_H = max(0.30, 3.1538/2 + 0.0955/2) = 1.6246
λ_A = max(0.30, 3.1538/2 − 0.0955/2) = 1.5292
Step 4 — Dixon-Coles PMF Grid (26×26)
formula: P(h,a) = τ(h,a,ρ) × Poisson(h; λ_H) × Poisson(a; λ_A), then normalise
τ(0,0)=1−λ_H×λ_A×ρ, τ(1,0)=1+λ_A×ρ, τ(0,1)=1+λ_H×ρ, τ(1,1)=1−ρ, τ(h,a)=1 for h+a≥2

τ(0,0) = 1 − 1.6246×1.5292×(-0.2000) = 1.4969

E[home goals] = 1.6246, E[away goals] = 1.5292

draw = Σ P(h,a) for h = a = 0.2783

formula: P(h,a) = τ(h,a,ρ) × Poisson(h; λ_H) × Poisson(a; λ_A), then normalise
τ(0,0)=1−λ_H×λ_A×ρ, τ(1,0)=1+λ_A×ρ, τ(0,1)=1+λ_H×ρ, τ(1,1)=1−ρ, τ(h,a)=1 for h+a≥2

formula: P(h,a) = τ(h,a,ρ) × Poisson(h; λ_H) × Poisson(a; λ_A), then normalise
τ(0,0)=1−λ_H×λ_A×ρ, τ(1,0)=1+λ_A×ρ, τ(0,1)=1+λ_H×ρ, τ(1,1)=1−ρ, τ(h,a)=1 for h+a≥2

margin = -0.4886 − 0.4749 = -0.9634

λ_A = max(0.30, 3.1538/2 − -0.9634/2) = 2.0586
Step 4 — Dixon-Coles PMF Grid (26×26)
formula: P(h,a) = τ(h,a,ρ) × Poisson(h; λ_H) × Poisson(a; λ_A), then normalise
τ(0,0)=1−λ_H×λ_A×ρ, τ(1,0)=1+λ_A×ρ, τ(0,1)=1+λ_H×ρ, τ(1,1)=1−ρ, τ(h,a)=1 for h+a≥2

τ(0,0) = 1 − 1.0952×2.0586×(-0.2000) = 1.4509

formula: P(h,a) = τ(h,a,ρ) × Poisson(h; λ_H) × Poisson(a; λ_A), then normalise
τ(0,0)=1−λ_H×λ_A×ρ, τ(1,0)=1+λ_A×ρ, τ(0,1)=1+λ_H×ρ, τ(1,1)=1−ρ, τ(h,a)=1 for h+a≥2
